Details of Chairman Chiang's Arrival in Jiangxi

Arrived in Xunyang on the Morning of the 7th, Arrived in the Province in the Afternoon

He Chengjun also arrived in Jiangxi from Hankou on the Same Day

Chiang Met with Party and Government Committee Members in Xunyang

Will Soon Go to Western Jiangxi to Plan Communist Suppression

Situation Upon Arrival in Jiujiang – Jiujiang Correspondence: Chairman Chiang set sail from Yong Sui warship at 10:00 PM on the 5th. The ship anchored at Hukou at 10:00 PM on the 6th, and set sail at dawn on the 7th, passing the Jinji Po Oil Depot Pier at 9:30 AM. Provincial Government Chairman Lu, along with Provincial Party Committee members Liu Zuozhou, Xiao Qian, Chen Gang, Gong Boxun, Provincial Government Committee members Lu Xiaochen, Huang Bozhong, Jiang Ji, Finance Special Commissioner Liu Hao, Wuhan Headquarters Representative Jia Botao, Sixth Route Commander-in-Chief Zhu's Representative Yu Zhen, Fifth Division Deputy Commander Yue Sen, Fifth Division Chief of Staff Guo Su, Ninth Route Headquarters Adjutant General Cao Xinbiao, High Court President Liang Renjie, Chief Prosecutor Hu Jue, and representatives from the Nanchang City Party Department, arrived at Xunyang from the province by special train at 3:00 PM on the 6th. They rushed to the riverfront pier of the San Bei Company at dawn on the 7th to welcome Chairman Chiang. The warship approached the pontoon at 9:45 AM. All Chinese and foreign warships stationed in Xunyang raised flags and fired twenty-one-gun salutes to pay respects. Representatives from all sectors of Jiujiang party, government, military, and civilian, numbering about a thousand, stood on the riverbank to welcome him. When the warship docked, the welcomers removed their hats and saluted. Military music played in unison. Along the river, guards and police stood in solemn salute. Chairman Chiang dispatched Secretary-General Shao Lizi and Director of the Political Training Department Zhou Fohai to go to the deck to thank the welcomers. He then summoned Chairman Lu, party and government committee members, and the High Court President. The security in Xunyang that day was extremely tight. Military police and sentries were densely deployed along the route from the riverfront pier to the train station. The Fifth Division, the Second Anti-Smuggling Regiment, and the Jiujiang Public Security Bureau's police team were responsible for different sections. In addition to sending the Chu You warship stationed in Hukou to escort the convoy, the Navy Department also dispatched the Minquan warship from Hankou on the evening of the 6th, led by Zeng Yiding, commander of the naval torpedo squadron, to Xunyang to assist the original Chu Qian warship in guarding the river. The Yong Sui warship that Chairman Chiang was on was decorated with party and national flags and various national silk flags. The decorations were extremely solemn. Chairman Chiang's accompanying personnel included Secretary-General Shao Lizi, Director of the Political Training Department Zhou Fohai, Chief of Staff Lin Wei, Secretary and Chief of the Confidential Section Xu Shitao, staff officers, adjutants, translators, and telegraph operators, totaling more than eighty people. In addition, guards, sentries, the eight departments of the Headquarters, the wireless team, and one platoon each of the telegraph and telephone teams, as well as the National Government Guard team, arrived in Xunyang at 8:00 AM on the 6th from Nanjing by the Jiang Tian and Yong Xing steamships. They then took a special train to the province in advance to make arrangements.

About fifteen minutes after Chairman Chiang arrived in Xunyang, He Chengjun also arrived in Xunyang from Hankou on the Chu Tai warship and boarded the Yong Sui warship to pay his respects to Chairman Chiang, reporting on the situation of communist suppression in Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi provinces, and welcoming Chairman Chiang to Hankou to give instructions on military and political affairs.

In the Yong Sui warship, Chairman Chiang first summoned Provincial Government Chairman Lu Dipin to inquire about everything, then summoned the provincial party and government committee members and High Court President, Fifth Division Deputy Commander Yue. Each committee member boarded the warship to pay their respects to Chairman Chiang and inquired about the provincial party and government situation.

Page 9

News Highlights

The following is a record of Chairman Chiang's meeting with party and government members. (1) Regarding party affairs: (1) Chairman Chiang asked if the organization of the lower-level party branches in Jiangxi was sound. Answer (Representative of the Provincial Party Branch Member Liu Zuozhou): Previously, the organization of party branches in more than ten counties in Jiangxi was quite unsound. After a period of reorganization, it is now sound. (2) Asked how the mass organizations in each county were. Answer: The Provincial Party Branch has formulated a plan for the mass organizations in each county, and three commissioners will be dispatched by the Provincial Party Branch to tour the counties and guide the party branches in each county to carry out the organization. (3) Asked how the Provincial Party Branch is currently working. Answer: Because three of the executive committee members have gone on tour, only three commissioners remain in the province, so the standing committee meeting has not been held. (4) Asked if party affairs in Ji'an have now been restored and how the mass movement is progressing. Answer: The county party branch commissioners in Ji'an were killed by bandits during the previous fall, and many staff members have fled Ji'an to avoid the bandits. Recently, after Ji'an was recovered, the Provincial Party Branch dispatched Commissioner Yin Jingrang to lead the county party affairs staff back to Ji'an to restore work. Because the degree of banditization of the Ji'an masses is relatively deep, the current party affairs work focuses on awakening the banditized masses, leading the masses to assist the army in clearing bandits, and organizing anti-communist groups and watch teams, etc. (2) Regarding political affairs: (1) Education Director Jiang Ji reported on the educational situation in the province, briefly stating that the education funds in the province have been affected by banditry, and the monthly funds are only set at 80,000 yuan, which is not enough to cover expenses, and education is on the verge of stagnation. He requested Chairman Chiang to maintain the original independence of the education fund, etc. Chairman Chiang nodded in agreement. (2) Finance Director Huang Bozhong reported on the financial situation in the province, briefly stating that the current financial difficulties in the province are beyond description. All expenditures are made by borrowing debts. In addition, at the present time, a large-scale bandit suppression is underway, and the funds for bandit suppression are still unsettled. He requested that Chairman Chiang not only allocate funds from the central government for subsidies, but also approve the central government to return to the province 3 million yuan of temporary exchange coupons exchanged in the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, and 3 million yuan for bandit suppression expenses and military rations that were advanced. Chiang replied, "Okay." (3) Liang Renjie, President of the High Court, reported on the judicial situation in the province. (4) Hu Jue, Chief Prosecutor of the High Court, reported on the disaster situation in Ji'an caused by bandits and requested the following three points: (A) Set a deadline for the army to thoroughly eliminate the bandits and communists in the province. (B) Clarify officialdom and punish corrupt officials. (C) Please allocate funds from the central government to relieve the victims of the disaster. (3)

Regarding military affairs: (1) Chairman Lu, who is also the commander-in-chief of the Ninth Route Army, reported on the progress of bandit suppression and the changes in the bandit situation. (2) Deputy Division Commander Yue of the 50th Division reported on the bandit suppression progress of the division and the current stationed location. Finally, Chairman Chiang met with the British and Japanese consuls stationed in Xunyang.

Chairman Chiang rested on the warship for a while. At 10:45 AM, he landed with He Chengjun, Shao Lizi, Zhou Fo Hai, and others. Amidst the military music and cheers of welcoming personnel, he rode in three cars with Chairman Lu and others directly to the station. All circles in Jiujiang originally planned to hold a welcoming meeting at Tongwen School and invite Chairman Chiang to attend and give a speech. Later, upon hearing that Chairman Chiang would not stay in Xunyang for a moment, they transferred from the riverfront to the station to see Chairman Chiang off. At 10:50 AM, he arrived at the station and boarded the special train, which was attached with thirteen first- and second-class carriages for the staff and welcoming personnel from the province to Xunyang to ride. The special train departed at 11:00 AM. The road-roller car departed at 10:00 AM, and the railway bureau telegraphed the troops along the road to pay attention to vigilance.

Situation upon arrival in Nanchang. Nanchang correspondent: Chairman Chiang's special train arrived at Niuhang Station at 3:15 PM on the afternoon of the 7th. At 3:30 PM, he crossed the river to the Provincial Library to stay. On that day, leaders and representatives of various institutions and organizations in Nanchang went to Zhangwai River in the morning starting at 6:00 AM to welcome him. They arrived one after another at noon. Zhu Shaoliang, commander-in-chief of the Sixth Route Army, Xiong Yanglin of the provincial government, the three provincial committees, and Mayor Gong and Zhang, the director of the Public Security Bureau, crossed the river to Niuhang Station to greet him. As for security matters, the 5th Division and the Independent 14th Brigade were stationed along the Nanxun Road. From Niuhang Station to the pontoon bridge across the Zhang River to the crossing point, the National Government Guard Regiment and a part of the 14th Brigade were on guard. From Yanjiang Road through Zhongshan Road to reach Baihuazhou, the 1st and 2nd Regiments of the Security Forces and the 1st, 2nd, and 3rd Squads of the Provincial Public Security Bureau Security Team were on guard. The road was cleared at around 10:00 AM, and those without welcome passes and symbols were not allowed to pass. When Chiang's special car started from Xunyang, the 9th Route Army also sent two Ke Sai planes to fly along the Nanxun Road and circle in the air to escort it. The strictness can be imagined.

When Chairman Chiang arrived at Niuhang Station, the military band played loudly. Zhu Shaoliang and others boarded the train to welcome him. Chiang got off the train and shook hands with the welcomers one by one. Together they boarded the American wheel to cross the river. When the wheel from the Road Bureau stopped at the landing point, a 21-gun salute was fired, the military music was melodious, the military police raised their guns, and the welcomers took off their hats to salute. After Chiang landed, he took off his hat to salute the welcoming crowds along the river. Then Chiang and his entourage took more than ten cars directly to the Provincial Library in Baihuazhou to stay. Lu Dipin and Zhu Shaoliang followed to pay their respects. It was heard that Chiang immediately convened a military conference at the province with He Chengjun and the two commanders-in-chief Lu and Zhu to discuss the specific plans for suppressing bandits in Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Fujian. It was also heard that Chiang, deeply moved by the devastation of western Jiangxi by the communists, decided to go to Ji'an with Commander Lu in the next few days to inspect and convene the division commanders Zhang, Tan, Xu, Deng, Gong, Luo, Chiang, and Cai to hold a military conference to discuss detailed methods of suppressing bandits in order to eliminate the bandits and communists within a time limit. (December 7th)

Preparations for Welcoming Chiang in Wuhan

Chiang scheduled to come to Wuhan on the 11th

Hankou correspondent: Commander-in-Chief Chiang took the Yong Sui warship west from Beijing on the 5th of this month and arrived in Xunyang on the 6th. After receiving the telegram, He Chengjun, head of the local headquarters, took the Chu Tai warship to Xunyang on the 6th to greet him. When he met with Commander-in-Chief Chiang on the 7th, Commander-in-Chief Chiang, along with his staff, He Chengjun, Lu Dipin, and others, departed from Xunyang. At noon, they arrived in Nanchang. Chiang, feeling that the bandit disaster in Jiangxi Province was more severe, specifically decided to convene a military conference in Nanchang on the 9th to discuss ways to eliminate the bandits in Jiangxi. He would return to Xunyang on the 11th and then transfer to Wuhan. He Chengjun planned to fly to Wuhan by plane on the 10th to make all the arrangements. All circles here have decided to hold a grand welcome when Chiang comes to suppress the bandits. The welcoming preparatory committee had previously issued many welcome badges. Recently, in order to be particularly cautious, it has published a notice in the newspaper to cancel the previously issued welcome badges and issue new ones by the Garrison Command. The Garrison Command has also re-specified the security and welcome methods, including: (1) Land security is the responsibility of the Wuhan Garrison Command's various martial law units, but the security area is divided into special security and general security. One, special security is from the landing dock of the Commander-in-Chief directly to the headquarters. Two, each branch road directly to the headquarters is a general security area. (2) The symbols for welcoming personnel are divided into special and general. One, special symbols are issued to military officers above the rank of major general and civil officials above the rank of senior official to pass through the special security line. Two, general symbols are issued to representatives of various agencies and organizations to pass outside the special security line. (3) The Wuhan Garrison Command will send personnel to strictly investigate and verify the symbols. One, investigate the security forces inside and outside the security area. Two, personnel or representatives wearing welcome symbols must clearly indicate their rank and name on the registration book before they can pass. Three, welcoming personnel or representatives wearing general symbols must not enter or leave the security line without authorization. Four, the registration book is set up at the main intersection of the general security line, and the symbol will be issued after registration. As for the fact that the road from the riverbank to the headquarters passes through the Japanese and French concessions, the municipal government has also contacted them and reached an agreement. On the one hand, our country's armed soldiers will enter the border to guard, and on the other hand, the concession authorities will still add posts to protect. It can also be seen that it is very strict.

As for the bandit suppression in Hubei Province, it has become more tense because Chiang came to Wuhan. The bandit communists in Huanggangkou, eastern Hubei, have been ordered by the headquarters to be eliminated by Guo Rudong and other troops within three days. Because the bandits have occupied the area for several months, all passing ships have been vigilant. If the bandit communists in this area are eliminated, the bandit nests in eastern Hubei will be breached. Secondly, Huang'an has been personally attacked by Xu Yuanquan and Xiao Zhichu, who have repeatedly defeated the bandit army. Xiao sent two telegrams to the headquarters on the 8th to report the victory. The text of the telegrams is as follows: (Telegram 1) (1) This division entered the Baliwan, 60 miles south of Huang'an today. (2) Wang Brigade advanced from Zhonghekou to the Daxiaojinshan area today and fought fiercely with more than a thousand communist bandits for a day, annihilating many bandits. (3) Xin Brigade is advancing from Changxianling to Shizidian Yaojiaji. (4) After Chen Brigade is transferred from Xin'an Baliwan, our division will use all its strength to attack Huang'an. Special report. (Telegram 2) 1. Zhang Shi's regiment of our Wang Brigade has driven away the Red Guards in Bancangdian Lijiawan Donglinpu and other places and is now occupying Kougongdian and other places, attacking Shen Changqian's bandits, who number about a thousand. Two. Chen Brigade Yu regiment has captured Dujialiangting and continued to search and suppress Gaopogang. Three. Xin Brigade Yang Xin regiment has retreated the Red Guards of Tal Mountain and continued to attack Shizidian. Li Yinshen regiment is advancing from Changxianling to Yaojiaji. Special report. (December 8th)

Establishment of the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission

Overseas Chinese Revolutionary Donation Investigation and Award Bureau

Overseas Chinese have donated a large amount of money to support the revolution of the motherland in the past. It is urgent to investigate and reward them to show their recognition. The central government previously accepted the suggestion of He Zhongying, the representative of the Singapore Tongde Newspaper, and handed over the investigation and awarding of this donation to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission. Later, it formulated four types of regulations, including the Regulations on the Investigation and Award of Overseas Chinese Revolutionary Donations, the Award Regulations, the Registration Rules, and the Bureau Regulations, and handed them over to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission for investigation and implementation. The association believed that the procedures for investigating and awarding this donation were very complicated, and that it would not be thorough unless a bureau was specifically set up to handle it. Therefore, according to Article 8 of the Regulations on the Investigation and Award of Overseas Chinese Revolutionary Donations, it established an Overseas Chinese Revolutionary Donation Investigation and Award Bureau under the association to be solely responsible for its affairs. The staff members were also transferred from the association's original staff to be responsible for the handling. It was officially established on the 1st of this month. The registration forms for the donation will be sent to the party branches, newspapers, and other overseas Chinese organizations that have historical relations with the Kuomintang in various places overseas to start the investigation for review and award separately.

Liaoning Provincial Government Decides to Set Up Police in Japanese Permanent Lease Land

Shenyang correspondent: The Liaoning Ning Provincial Government previously received a report from the Commercial Port Public Security Bureau stating that there were several permanent lease lands in the boundary, including Inoue Nobuo, Hirano Masaaki, Kamata Yasuke, and the 12 Biaochun sections, covering a large area. In the past, due to special circumstances or unresolved negotiations, police stations had not been added to all these lands. According to the port regulations, although the land is permanently leased by the Japanese, sovereignty belongs to our country, and police posts should be established as soon as possible to maintain law and order and prevent guests from taking over the host. It requested the Provincial Public Security Bureau to make proper arrangements to maintain sovereignty. The provincial government ordered the special commissioner for foreign affairs to review it. Then, according to the reply, the commercial port area of the provincial capital is a self-opened commercial port. Although foreigners are allowed to lease it permanently, sovereignty is entirely ours. The original report listed the large sections of permanent lease land of Japanese Inoue Nobuo, Hirano Masaaki, Kamata Yasuke, and 12 Biaochun. Except for the 12 Biaochun, which has been negotiated and our country has set up posts, the relevant bureaus and volumes have been consulted in other places, and the clauses signed with the Japanese Hirano and Kamata, etc., stipulate that public land, police stations, etc. are all reserved for use by the bureau, so there is no problem. The Inoue Nobuo item is for Sun Huichuan to change his name to receive the tenant. Although no other clauses have been signed, it must comply with the port regulations and should be handled in the same way. Although most of the land is currently undeveloped and relatively empty, it is beneficial to prevent thieves and is of great benefit to the ground. After receiving the report, the provincial government has now ordered Bai Mingzhen, director of the Provincial Public Security Bureau, to set up police stations in each of these places as soon as possible. (December 4th)

Full Text of the Civil Code Kinship Section (4) (Continued)

Chapter 3 Parents and Children (Article 1059) Children follow the father's surname. The children of the groom follow the mother's surname, but if there is another agreement, it will follow the agreement. (Article 1060) The domicile of minor children is the domicile of their parents. The domicile of the children of the groom is the domicile of their mother. (Article 1061) Children born in wedlock are children conceived during the marriage relationship. (Article 1062) The period from 181 days before the child's date of birth to 302 days is the period of conception. If it can be proven that conception can be traced back to before the aforementioned 302 days, that period shall be the period of conception. (Article 1063) If a wife's conception occurs during the continuation of the marriage relationship, it is presumed that the children she bears are children born in wedlock. If the husband can prove that he did not cohabit with his wife during the period of conception, he may file a suit for denial, but he must do so within one year from the date he learns of the child's birth. (Article 1064) Non-marital children who are married by their biological father and mother are regarded as children born in wedlock. (Article 1065) Non-marital children who are recognized by their biological father are regarded as children born in wedlock. Those who are raised by their biological father are regarded as recognized. The relationship between non-marital children and their biological mother is regarded as children born in wedlock and does not require recognition. (Article 1066) The biological mother of a non-marital child can deny the recognition of her biological father. (Article 1067) In one of the following circumstances, the biological mother or other legal representative of a non-marital child may request the biological father to recognize it: (1) The biological father and mother had cohabitation during the period of conception. (2) A document made by the biological father can prove that he is the biological father. (3) The biological mother was raped or abducted by the biological father. (4) The biological mother was sexually assaulted by the biological father's abuse of power. The aforementioned right to request shall expire if it is not exercised within five years after the child's birth. (Article 1068) If the biological mother has had adultery with others or a dissolute life during the period of conception, the provisions of the preceding article shall not apply. (Article 1069) The effect of a non-marital child's 7

Page 10

price shall be retroactive to the time of birth, but the rights already obtained by a third party shall not be affected thereby. (Article 1070) A biological father may not revoke his recognition after recognizing a non-marital child. (Article 1071) When an heir is designated in accordance with the provisions of Article 1145, the relationship between the heir and the decedent shall be the same as that of a child born in wedlock, unless otherwise provided by law. (Article 1072) When adopting another person's child as a child, the adopter is the adoptive father and adoptive mother, and the adoptee is the adopted son or adopted daughter. (Article 1073) The age of the adopter should be 20 years or more older than that of the adoptee. (Article 1074) When a person with a spouse adopts a child, he should do so jointly with his spouse. (Article 1075) Except as provided in the preceding article, a person may not be the adopted child of two people at the same time. (Article 1076) A person with a spouse should obtain the consent of his spouse when being adopted. (Article 1077) The relationship between adopted children and adoptive parents shall be the same as that of children born in wedlock, unless otherwise provided by law. (Article 1078) Adopted children follow the surname of the adopter. (Article 1079) The adoption of children should be in writing, but this does not apply to those who have been raised as children since childhood. (Article 1080) The relationship between adoptive parents and adopted children may be terminated with the consent of both parties. The aforementioned termination should be in writing. (Article 1081) If one of the adoptive parents or adopted children has one of the following circumstances, the court may declare the termination of the adoption relationship at the request of the other party: (1) When he commits abuse or serious insults against the other party. (2) When he maliciously abandons the other party. (3) When the adopted child is sentenced to imprisonment for two years or more. (4) When the adopted child wastes property. (5) When the life or death of the adopted child is unknown for more than three years. (6) When there are other major reasons. (Article 1082) When the adoption relationship is terminated by a judgment, the party who is not at fault and is therefore in financial difficulty may request the other party to give a considerable amount of money. (Article 1083) Adopted children shall restore their original surname from the time the adoption relationship is terminated and restore their relationship with their biological parents, but the rights already acquired by a third party shall not be affected thereby. (Article 1084) Parents have the right and obligation to protect and educate their minor children. (Article 1085) Parents may discipline their children within the necessary scope. (Article 1086) Parents are the legal representatives of their minor children. (Article 1087) Property acquired by minor children through inheritance, donation, or other free means is their special property. (Article 1088) The special property of children is managed by the father. If the father cannot manage it, it is managed by the mother. Parents have the right to use and benefit from their children's special property, but they may not dispose of it unless it is for the benefit of the children. (Article 1089) The rights and obligations of minor children shall be exercised or borne jointly by the parents, unless otherwise provided by law. When parents disagree on the exercise of rights, they shall be exercised by the parents. When one of the parents is unable to exercise their rights, the other party shall exercise them. When parents cannot jointly bear obligations, they shall be borne by those who are able. (Article 1090) When parents abuse their rights over their children, their closest relatives or a family meeting may correct them. If the correction is invalid, they may request the court to declare the suspension of all or part of their rights.

Chapter 4 Guardianship Section 1 Guardianship of Minors (Article 1091) If a minor has no parents, or both parents are unable to exercise their rights and obligations over their minor children, a guardian should be appointed, but this does not apply to minors who are already married. (Article 1092) Parents may entrust others to exercise the duties of guardianship for their minor children for a specific matter within a certain period of time. (Article 1093) The father or mother who dies later may designate a guardian in their will. (To be continued)

Local Correspondences

Songjiang

After interrogating the Tinglin communist prisoners, it was found that Pu'nan Hougang Mapengdianshan and other places were all places where the Songjin connection was active as communists. They often gathered openly for meetings at night as a common practice. Although the local people heard about it, they did not dare to report it. Yesterday, when the county police team was stationed in Hougang, they captured an important element sent from another place to work there. The county government dispatched Political Police Chief Dong Futang to Tinglin to bring him back. The county government committee member Du interrogated the prisoner, who confessed that his name was Gu Zhigao from Chongming Yilongzhen. He used to be a partner in the Shenshengnan Goods Store in Shanghai Baxianqiao. He was laid off in May. This time, he went to Lvgang to visit a friend. On the train, he met another friend who sent him a rattan basket. He didn't meet his friend and was arrested on the way back. The confession was cunning. The interrogating officer ordered him to be detained. It was heard that the list of party members stored in the rattan basket included several people living in Tinglin Town, such as Yang. By the time they went to search, they had all fled upon hearing the news. Speakers said that the bandit was not without status in the party there.

The Education Bureau added a People's Education Center. The Education Bureau believes that popular education is a priority during the period of political tutelage. A popular education center has been established in Tinglin and has been quite successful. Fengjing is also an important town in the county and it is necessary to establish a People's Education Center. The Bureau Affairs Meeting has decided to add one in Fengjing and has ordered Shen Fuyun, the principal of the Third Elementary School, to prepare.

Inspector Zheng handed over his duties and left office. Zheng Han, the inspector of the Sixth Sub-Station in Sijing, is a native of Fengjing. He has served in the area for seven years and has a very good relationship with the local people. This time, after receiving the news that he was transferred back for use, they unanimously submitted a request to retain him. However, Inspector Zheng was determined to break away because of his lack of energy and decided to transfer the official seals, public property, and documents to the successor before waiting for approval, and scheduled to hire a boat to return to Feng on the 9th of this month.

Nanhui

Continued interrogation of the Sun Jingqing conflict with the saltworks. Sun Jingqing, the education committee member of the Second District of this county, had a conflict with the Xiassha Saltworks Office for taking Tandan on behalf of others. It is now known that Sun did not appear in court on the 20th of last month because the case was due to be heard, because he hoped that someone would mediate or settle the matter, so he filed a request for an extension. A certain important person at sea did write to the saltworks at that time, requesting a peaceful resolution, but the saltworks did not show any willingness to accommodate, so the matter has been delayed until now. Yesterday was the date for the continued summons for interrogation. Sun arrived in court and Lu, the trial officer, briefly interrogated him for a few words, and also instructed Sun to quickly ask someone to mediate and settle the matter, otherwise he would only have to deal with it according to law. The Provincial Education Department also insisted on handling the case according to law. The county government received this order yesterday, ordering them to comply immediately.

The president of the public hospital was replaced. Zhang Jianqian, the president of the First Public Hospital of this county, recently repeatedly submitted a request to the county government to resign because he was not familiar with medical skills and was deeply afraid of delaying hospital affairs. The board of directors of the hospital held a meeting yesterday and decided to hire Western doctor Lin Yuqing as the president. They have submitted a request to the county government for approval.

Fengxian

The two branches of the Jianyuan temple, one for renovation and one for construction. After the Fenggao Court sent personnel to order the renovation of the Jianyuan temple in this county, the county union organized the Jianyuan Temple Fundraising Committee to handle the matter in Fengcheng. The people from all circles in the west of the township believed that the old prison in Fengcheng was dilapidated and unsuitable, and that the Yue sacrifices had been dangerous many times. Therefore, they advocated building a new prison in Nanhqiao, where the county seat is located, in order to make it complete. Jiang Rongchu, the chief of the First, Fifth, Sixth, Seventh, and Eighth districts, was appointed to prepare reasons to telegraph the High Court, ordering the county to stop the renovation and allow the people to automatically raise 12,000 yuan to start construction as soon as possible. Subsequently, they were approved to submit a report stating that building a new prison in the county seat was a good idea, but whether the funds had been settled and how the project would be carried out should be reported in detail before approval could be given. The people in the east of the township heard this news and rose up in opposition, and Chen Daiji, a member of the renovation fundraising committee, sent a letter to the High Court asking Shi Zechen, the original investigator, for instructions. Their reason was that Feng county was narrow and long, and the distance between east and west was extremely far. The east of the township relied on this judicial organ to suppress it. Once it moved to the west, the security would be worrying. In addition, the people's livelihood was declining, and considering the situation and reason, renovation was the most economical. It is now known that the committee has submitted the case to the High Court, which ordered the county to check the county on the 4th. The fundraising renovation of the prisons in the county was based on the expansion of the existing old prisons in the city and there was no order to build a new prison in the county seat. It was a misunderstanding that they should immediately order the county chief to work with the fundraising committee to report the fundraising results in detail along with the engineering estimate of the construction factory, and start work on the appointed day so that the success could be observed as soon as possible. The districts should not use excuses to delay prison administration. Therefore, the committee officially recruited workers to undertake the construction yesterday, and the money for the insufficient donations was discussed to dismantle the city bricks of the east and west Yongmen and supplement the sages in Pat. The deadline was set to complete the repairs within two months. However, the construction of the new prisons in the west of the township is still actively underway, and the initiators have recognized and paid for the exploration of the Yizhong site behind the county government to prepare for construction. The two sides are at a stalemate and it is feared that it will not be easy to resolve it for a while.

Suzhou

Highwaymen in Hushan Township injured people. Mao Xiaobao, a villager in Anxiu Village near Dongqiao Town in Hushan Township, which belongs to the county, was about to get married the day before yesterday. There were many guests on that day. All the guests had left at about 11:00 PM that night. Unexpectedly, fifteen or sixteen bandits suddenly came in with weapons and robbed them, taking away about 500 yuan. The bandits then went to the homes of Zhu Xiuzheng, Zhu Tongchun, and Zhu Xiaobao to search and rob them, and shot and injured two farmers before fleeing.

The thief who robbed the bracelet and injured someone was arrested. The case of Chen Wang, a woman at No. 19, the first Tianmen of Guanqian Palace Lane, being robbed of a gold bracelet by thugs and Han Xueliang, a passerby, being stabbed on the evening of the 7th was solved that night after Director Zou of the Public Security Bureau notified all subordinates to assist in the arrest. At about 6:00 PM on the evening before (the 8th), Xu Dexing, the chief of the Criminal Investigation Team, together with investigators Shi Runhan and Yang Fushan, arrested the perpetrator Yu Asan in the Jinjiang First Building teahouse in Qianmen Neigao Bridge. They immediately took the team to investigate and interrogate him. He confessed to the robbery and injury without hesitation and was transferred to the Public Security Bureau for transfer to the local court for verification yesterday (the 9th).

Ma Wenxiang and his grandson were kidnapped and rescued in Houbao Town, Xishan, Dongting. After Ma Wenxiang and his grandson were kidnapped by bandits on the 11th of last month, Wang Wusheng, the captain of the 8th Water Public Security Team, ordered Zhu Deming, the deputy captain of the 2nd Team stationed in Xishan, to solve the case within a time limit. Zhu, the deputy captain, led a boat to patrol behind Qushan on the day before (the 8th) and caught a glimpse of several bandit boats. He immediately fired with platoon guns. The bandits, seeing that the situation was not good, abandoned their tickets in the lake and escaped. Zhu rescued the hostages, the Ma family grandfather and grandson, and brought them back to the team headquarters. However, the bandit boats were able to escape.

Wuxi

The Establishment of the County Court is Near: The Wuxi County Court building has already been completely repaired. President Lin of the Jiangsu High Court has decided to formally establish it on January 1st of next year. As for the selections of the court president, chief prosecutor, judges, and chief secretary, President Lin has already internally determined them and will announce them soon. The County Court building project is also scheduled to have the Prison Section Chief Secretary and County Court Preparatory Member Yao Guozhang dispatched to Wuxi the day after tomorrow to jointly inspect and accept it with the county government. Yesterday, it was learned that County Magistrate Pan Zhongjia, considering that the establishment of the County Court is near and the days of the county concurrently handling judicial matters are dwindling, instructed the staff of the adjudication office to sort, bind, and make detailed inventories of all concluded and unconcluded civil and criminal case files in preparation for handover to the County Court for handling. Furthermore, Chief of Political Affairs Police Wu Zhengrong received a handwritten order from County Magistrate Pan, instructing him to immediately inform all political affairs police officers who wish to remain in the county government or go to the County Court as bailiffs to submit their written applications, clearly stating their intentions, by 9:00 AM on the 9th, and to submit them to Chief Wu for compilation and reporting to the County for forwarding to the High Court for approval.

Another Arrest in the Xiaoqiaotou Robbery Case: Shen Kunquan's home, a resident of Xiaoqiaotou near Dai Qi in the Fifth District (Tianshang City) of the county, was broken into by seven or eight bandits last winter, who conducted a large-scale search and robbery, resulting in significant losses. After police investigation, a bandit named Yin Shungen was apprehended in this case and escorted to the county for interrogation and detention. It is now learned that Lei Jiaju, Chief of the 13th Sub-Bureau of the Fifth District Public Security Bureau, instructed police officers Zhang Weishu and Yuan Pei'en, among others, to patrol Yeqiao Town at 12:00 AM the day before yesterday. When they saw a suspicious person loitering, they immediately went forward, apprehended him, and brought him to the bureau. After preliminary interrogation by Chief Lei, he confessed his name as Li Guanlin, 30 years old, living in Changxiang of this county and working as a cook. He also confessed that he and Yin Shungen, Zhang A'zuo, and others, eight people in total, robbed Shen Kunquan's house, sharing the loot of one silver dollar, etc. Chief Lei recorded his confession and immediately prepared a document yesterday to escort him to the County Public Security Bureau to await transfer to the County for strict handling.

Construction of the Xiyi Road Commences: The Xiyi Provincial Road, constructed by the Construction Bureau, held a groundbreaking ceremony on the 1st of this month. The first section (from Meiyuan starting point to Yixing, totaling four sections) commenced construction on the 6th. On the first day of construction, the requisitioned villagers were quite enthusiastic, with more than a thousand people participating and the work progressing smoothly. Therefore, it is expected that the earthworks of the road can be completed within the year to facilitate transportation. Wang Wei, Captain of the Traffic Police Brigade, also selected eight police officers the day before yesterday, equipped with firearms, led by Patrol Chief Qin Shuwang, to protect the road construction workers.

Armed Robbery and Injury Case in Dongdupu Town: The Changdang Lake area in Jintan County is vast and the defenses are weak. Previously, approval was obtained from the Provincial Government's Department of Civil Affairs and Security Office to order the Second Water Police District to dispatch shallow-water gunboats to patrol the area. A few days ago, more than twenty bandits suddenly arrived in Dongdupu Town, armed with broadswords, box cannons, and other weapons. They first confiscated the firearms of the defense corps, then looted the entire town, killing two people and wounding two others with gunfire. Before leaving, they kidnapped seven people and fled by boat towards the Da'ang Mountain area. Yesterday, County Magistrate Zhu Ting of the county sent a letter to Mao Mujun, District Chief of the Second Water Police District, requesting the swift dispatch of three patrol boats to garrison the lake entrance to provide security.

Surtax Remittance to the Province Affects Bureau Funding: The County Government previously received an order from the province that all surtax penalties for late grain tax payments from this year's spring harvest must be remitted to the province in full. County Magistrate Pan repeatedly submitted the difficult situation to the provincial government, requesting that half be remitted to the province and half remain for county use. However, the provincial government has not approved this request because it concerns a general case. Recently, the Construction Bureau stated that the bureau's fixed monthly operating expenses are 260 yuan. In addition to the allocation from the six-fen land tax, the remainder is paid from the industrial expenses, with the allocation from surtax penalties for late grain tax payments accounting for about half. For example, the late fee surtax for the spring grain of 143,942 taels is calculated as 50% over the limit, with an additional levy of 2 jiao and 5 li per tael, totaling silver 14,754 yuan. The late fee for the winter grain of 75,466 shi is calculated as 50% over the limit, with an additional levy of 5 jiao per shi, totaling silver 18,867 yuan. The late fee surtax for reed tax of 349 taels is calculated as 50% over the limit, with an additional levy of 2 jiao and 5 li, totaling silver 357 yuan. If half of the above three items are remitted to the province and half are retained, the Construction Bureau should account for 26%, of which two-thirds totals silver 2,917 yuan. If all of it is remitted to the province, the Construction Bureau's operating expenses will inevitably be affected. Yesterday, a request was specially submitted to the County Government to offset it from the Construction Special Tax to be forwarded for approval to provide relief.

Changshu

A Proclamation for Rectifying the Long-Standing Malpractices of the Judiciary: County Magistrate Tan, considering the prevalence of lawsuits in the local area and the litigious nature of the people compared to other counties, issued a proclamation with the following text: "Since taking office, this magistrate has heard that the long-standing malpractices of the judiciary in Changshu have not been thoroughly rectified. Therefore, judicial personnel have been repeatedly warned to maintain integrity and uphold the dignity of the judiciary to avoid criticism. All judicial police and clerical staff are also paid salaries and must not make demands outside. This magistrate, in order to strengthen rectification, constantly supervises the adjudicators and others to handle litigation matters impartially and without prejudice. All litigants must be straightforward and present the facts truthfully in court, and the matter will be impartially adjudicated based on the law. If anyone dares to attempt bribery to confuse right and wrong, they will be severely punished without leniency once verified. If there are any lawless persons who dare to use this as an excuse to solicit fees, the victim should immediately report to the nearest public security sub-bureau or stationed office to arrest and bring them to the government for strict investigation. However, no one should make false accusations out of spite, causing inconvenience."

Disturbances Occur Again in Xiyang Town: Due to the repeated kidnappings and robberies in Xiyang Town in the Fushan District of this county, the residents in nearby areas such as Jincun are all in constant anxiety. Whenever a warning is received, they panic. At about 9:00 PM the night before last, five pirate ships appeared off the coast of Xiyang. The police stationed there immediately reported by telephone to Miaoqiao and Jincun that five pirate ships had arrived off the coast, but it was unknown where they were heading. Upon hearing the news, the residents of the town fled in droves. Within minutes, Jincun received another phone call stating that the bandits had landed with weapons and were advancing towards the area, urging them to be on alert. Upon receiving this information, the Jincun Business Corps immediately armed themselves with live ammunition and maintained strict vigilance. The merchants and residents of Jincun were also at a loss, and women even went down to the boats to flee. Then, after discussions among the people, stationed police, and the business corps, they decided to take precautions. Around 3:00 AM, they received a call from Miaoqiao stating that a public security team had gone to Xiyang Town, inflicting heavy casualties on the bandits, who had retreated. Only then did the people calm down a bit, but they had already been greatly alarmed.

Changzhou

Military, Police, and Militia Winter Defense Meeting: The Wuyi Military, Police, and Militia Joint Defense Office held a winter defense meeting at Fangsheng Temple at 2:00 PM on the 8th. Ren Chengren, commander of the Second Gendarmerie Regiment and director of the office, presided over the meeting. He reported that the third battalion of his unit had been approved by Commander Xiong to be stationed in Wujin, and was expected to arrive around the 9th. He also described the importance of this year's winter defense. The following proposals were then discussed: (1) It was resolved to send a letter to the Transport Battalion requesting it to join the winter defense and to dispatch a team to be stationed inside and outside Xiaobei and Zhengwang Temple, along with the Fourth Stationed Office, for permanent defense. (2) It was resolved that the Third Gendarmerie Battalion would be responsible for strict patrols in the Fourth and Fifth Districts. (3) It was resolved to divide the entire city into seven defense zones, and the county would instruct the town offices to find seven housing locations, with ten to twenty gendarmes stationed at each location. (4) It was resolved to send a letter to each rear hospital prohibiting wounded soldiers from going out at night. (5) It was resolved to strictly crack down on discharged wounded soldiers who linger and collude with hooligans.

Bandit Wu Boyuan Arrested in Weicun: Wu Boyuan, a bandit from Tianye Village in the Fourth District of Wuyi County, recently gathered his accomplices Shang Changsheng, Zhou the Little Monk, etc., and kidnapped the seven-year-old son of his nephew-in-law Xue Bingsheng and hid him at home, demanding a large ransom. The victim had already redeemed him. However, Wu Boyuan arrived at Weicun the night before last and hid in the Binjiang Hotel. He was apprehended by Jiang Hanying, chief of the Fourth Sub-Bureau of the town's public security, who led the police to search the inn. After interrogation, he confessed to the details of the incident. He was escorted to the City Public Security Bureau on the 8th for interrogation and detention.

Jiangyin

Suspects in Zhou Case Still Need to Be Arrested: In the Zhou Shuiping case, related suspects Zhang Wen, Yang Shao Cheng, Zhang Wufeng, Zhang Bu Lan, Zhu Zhenyang and others had been declared innocent by the court this spring, and all of them had returned to their villages. Zhou Zhongfu, Zhou Shuiping's father, recently submitted another petition to the provincial government regarding the death of his son Zhou Shuiping, urging that the 32nd resolution be consulted and that the Jiangyin county magistrate be ordered to implement it according to law. In addition, the fake attachment should be revoked to conclude the case. The province approved that since the case had been repeatedly submitted by the people, a letter had been sent to the provincial party rectification committee to convene a review as soon as possible, and the investigation results would be discussed to conclude the case. Also, a letter was sent to the National Government's Civil Service Department, urging the investigation and asking them to wait for the handling. The Jiangyin County Party Rectification Committee also held its 47th committee meeting the day before yesterday. Because the Zhou case was in the final stage of resolution by both the provincial party and government agencies, and the wanted criminals had returned to their hometowns, they should be arrested and brought to justice before a resolution is reached to show justice. Yesterday, a letter was sent to the county for handling. After approving the letter, County Magistrate Li ordered the Public Security Bureau to strictly implement it.

Ji and Cai are Remitted to the Province but Not Yet Interrogated: Zhu Xingnan (alias Wang Chuntao) from Xiagang was arrested in Suzhou and remitted to the province but has not yet been tried. Ji Hehua and Cai Rushan were remitted to the province, and there are many cases in the military law office but have not yet been interrogated. Ji's mother and wife live in Zhenjiang waiting for news. It is said that the military law office plans to move into the old garrison yamen on Wutiao Street to facilitate matters. Recently, rumors have been circulating in Jiangyin that Wei and Cai have already been executed, which is completely unfounded.

Zhenjiang

Zheng Chengyuan Confirmed to Have Accepted Bribes in the Liyang Corruption Case: The Zhenjiang Court has repeatedly studied the Liyang land tax corruption case. The day before yesterday, in addition to the first court session to investigate the original plaintiffs Di Shao Chen, Di Fu and Song Mo, the second investigation involved Lu Zhenglin, Zhao Dianhua and Lu Ziven, three old bookkeepers newly summoned from Liyang. After questioning, they were sent to detention. The third time, the five detainees Shi Taorong, Shi Qingyun, Hu Jinghua, Di Hongxun and Ren Shusen were brought to court for investigation until 7 o'clock before being ordered to return to detention. After dinner, another investigation court was opened, and Prosecutor Yan signed an order to bring the six detainees Zheng Chengyuan, Pan Bin, Huang Xingan, Shen Zhiqing, Zhou Shi and Cao Qingan to court for interrogation. After questioning each of them for a long time, although Zheng relied on his eloquence and hoped to escape the law, Mr. Yan had secretly investigated in Liyang and obtained ironclad evidence of bribery, as well as strong witnesses to prove the circumstances. In previous court sessions, Zheng had been high-spirited and seemed to be full of grievances, but after yesterday's court session, his attitude suddenly changed and he seemed ashamed. The interrogation ended late at night and he was ordered to return to detention. It is said that the case will be conducted in two parts: one is the case of Zheng receiving a bribe of 6,000 yuan, and the other is the land tax corruption case. The general situation of the bribery case has been investigated clearly and will be submitted for trial first. The land tax situation is complicated, and the main person in charge, former county magistrate Zhang Quan, is still at large, so it is feared that the case will be difficult to conclude in the shortest possible time.

County Magistrates Who Passed the Exam Will Go to Various Counties to Investigate: The 19 county magistrates who passed the second exam in Jiangsu Province have completed their training in the province. The provincial government now plans to divide them into groups of two and send them to various counties for investigation. After returning to the province, they will be assigned to various counties to take office.

High Assets Gang Broke: The Sixth Division of the National Army stationed in the province, the 31st Regiment, Commander Ding, sent Wu and Wang, two battalion commanders, to lead their teams to suppress the High Assets Gang. Yesterday, Battalion Commander Wang captured Chen Kuanchun and other four well-known bandit leaders in Xijishan, killed six or seventy people, and captured the bandits who have been sent to the regiment headquarters for interrogation. The Provincial Government Guard Battalion Went to Su to Suppress Bandits: Shen Jianhao, Battalion Commander of the Jiangsu Provincial Government Guard Battalion, was ordered to lead two platoons of armed soldiers with dozens of box cannons to Suzhou last night by walking to the train station and attaching three iron-covered cars drawn by the Railway Bureau to train 208 to Suzhou to strip bandits.

Construction Bonds Are Not Allowed to Be Reduced or Exempted: The Jiangsu Provincial Government issued 7 million yuan in construction bonds, and the regulations for distributing and using the funds have been drafted and submitted to the National Government for approval. Recently, a small number of counties have had citizens who have misunderstood the situation and directly petitioned the provincial government to request exemption or reduction of the allocated bonds. They have been approved separately. Now, Commissioners Chen, Hu, and Sun have proposed that citizens from four counties, including Wuxian, etc., petition for exemption from the construction bonds and request that the county magistrates of the four counties be strictly ordered to be responsible for persuading and guiding them to facilitate the progress. The case was resolved to be handled accordingly.

Nantong

Large Gangs of Pirates Invade Lvsi: On the 8th, more than 30 pirate ships suddenly arrived off the coast of Lvsi, with 700-800 pirates, who bombarded the shore, causing merchants and residents to flee. County Magistrate Zhang immediately dispatched police to block and rescue them. The question of the selection of the director of the relief institute is that the Nantong relief institute is the merger and reorganization of the original charitable organizations. The county government has appointed Zhao Jianhua to explain that local people from all walks of life have publicly recommended the director, expressing their opposition.

Yangzhou

Dispute over a Married Woman Remarrying: Yao Ruilin, who resides in Jiuxiang in this city, joined the army several years ago due to difficult circumstances. His wife gave birth to a child and, unable to make a living, was introduced by a matchmaker to work as a wet nurse at the Yu residence on Yinshi Street. Before long, she had an affair with the Yu family's male servant, Ding Deyuan. After she was no longer needed as a wet nurse, she moved in with Ding after her husband did not return. They lived together as husband and wife and asked Wang and Li and Sun Yutang's wife to witness. Yao Ruilin suddenly returned home the day before yesterday and learned that his wife had remarried Ding. He reported the situation to the First Public Security Bureau and requested that they help him reclaim his wife. It is unknown how this will be resolved.

Embezzlement of Public Funds and Escape: Xu Bingquan, the former cashier used by Director Yu of the County Finance Bureau, embezzled the land registration fees and other revenues collected from various district offices, as well as the related payment documents. When the current Director Tong took office, he did not receive these payments. Therefore, he sent a letter urging the district offices to recover the money, but the district offices said they had already paid and had receipts as proof. It is now said that Director Tong has been investigating and pursuing former Director Yu.

Gaoyou

Detectives Rescue Little Hostages: Xu Bin, a detective from the Sixth District of the Provincial Public Security Team stationed in You Shui, and others encountered bandits on the way to Linze Town to investigate a case the day before yesterday. Xu and others opened fire and the bandits returned fire and fled north, leaving behind two hostage boys, one named Chen He and one named Gao Yuzi. They were immediately taken to the district headquarters. It is now heard that the families of the two children, Chen Zhou and Gao Youxiang, have come to the city to claim them.

Each District Organizes District Regiments: County Magistrate Wang, believing that the four townships are not peaceful and bandits are everywhere, and that the original defense corps are mostly nominal, specially convened a meeting of the district chiefs the other day to have the original defense corps taken over by the district offices and renamed district regiments. The district heads of each district have been appointed by the county government. Currently, each district is actively recruiting militia and raising funds to purchase guns and ammunition, and it is expected that they will all be organized by the end of the year.

Chief of the Third Section of the Public Security Bureau Arrested: Li Ruomeng, Chief of the Third Section of the Public Security Bureau of this county, was arrested at 6:00 PM today (the 7th) while smoking opium at the home of a prostitute named Xiao Yazi in the south of the North City Jesus Church. The police task force learned of this and sent Peng Shiliang and others to arrest him on the spot. He was sent to the county government along with the smoking paraphernalia for legal action.

Yangzhong

Continued Report on the Robbery Case at Dongxinggang: It is now learned that the robbery at Dongxinggang in Yangzhong on the evening of the 5th was carried out against passengers on the Deda Company's steamer. While the steamer was docked, 20 to 30 bandits boarded under the guise of inspection and robbed them, resulting in a total loss of about 100 yuan.

County Magistrate Celebrates Birthday with a Big Feast for Guests: Yesterday (the 6th) was the 30th birthday of Xu Zusheng, the county magistrate of Yangzhong. After the departure of Zhu Hejun of the Provincial Committee (the Provincial Committee was investigating a case in Yang), a birthday hall was set up in the county government, and officials and local gentry went to congratulate him. County Magistrate Xu held a banquet at the government to thank the guests for their good wishes.

Request for Thorough Investigation of Fabricated Banditry Case: Wang Xin of Baziqiao in Yangzhong County once served as an executive member of the County Party Department and a primary school principal. However, due to his upright nature, he has incurred much resentment in the local area and has been repeatedly falsely accused and imprisoned. He was eventually acquitted after someone proved his innocence. Recently, he was falsely accused by local bullies such as Shi Yicheng of colluding with bandits and dividing stolen goods. The Provincial Department of Civil Affairs ordered the county government to investigate and arrest him. Upon hearing the news, local party members, feeling that a loyal comrade had been falsely accused again and again, had Guo and others submit a petition to the authorities requesting that the plaintiffs be summoned to court for a thorough investigation.

Huzhou

Robbery and Kidnapping Occurs in Changxing and Zhu Er Qian, Hu City: Zhu Er Qian, the local resident twelve miles away from Dadongmen outside Changxing, and Lan Gou Nian, who are in their seventies, are slightly wealthy. Li believes that the bandits are rampant there, so he moved to the city in the spring to take shelter temporarily. Now, when Di is harvested, the whole family returns to the countryside to take care of farming affairs. The bandits learned about it and suddenly came at about 10:00 PM on the 5th of this month. More than twenty bandits with a local accent were all holding guns and other weapons, broke into the house and robbed all the clothes, ornaments and cash, with a loss of more than 500 yuan. Li's daughter-in-law and two grandsons were also taken away, leaving a letter demanding a huge amount of money.

The Gendarmerie Battalion Departs Changxing to Transfer to Suhu: Since the bandits spread to the western townships of Huzhou, the Third Battalion of the Second Gendarmerie Regiment was dispatched by the central government to Changxing to assist the military and police in capturing bandits this spring. It has now received an order from the regimental headquarters to be transferred to Jiangsu Province. The local defense in that area is now being guarded by soldiers dispatched by the security team of this city.

Jiaxing

The County Farmers' Association Stops Activities: The Jiaxing County Farmers' Association has been established after being reorganized, and the members are working hard to carry out the planned work. It is now learned that the backbone members of the association have been accused by someone to the Provincial Executive Committee. After receiving the report, the Provincial Executive Committee ordered the County Executive Committee to investigate and reply. Therefore, the County Executive Committee decided at its 66th meeting on the 8th to order the County Farmers' Association to stop activities immediately, and the association will send personnel to take over the handling. At the same time, the training department will directly manage the district and township farmers' associations as usual. The actual situation of the farmers' associations at all levels will be carefully investigated by the recruitment and examination staff when they are dispatched to various districts and a report will be submitted to the Provincial Executive Committee for verification.

Recent News on the Construction Corruption Case at the Business School: The case of construction corruption at the Jiaxing Business School has been repeatedly reported by local people, but the authorities have not taken effective measures, resulting in the embezzlement of more than 10,000 yuan of public funds. The year before last, Zhou Guoxun and other local citizens filed a complaint with the court, and the relevant persons were summoned for questioning. Because a certain person, the most important person involved, had left, the evidence was insufficient and the court ruled that no prosecution would be pursued. Zhou Guoxun, believing that the matter concerned public funds and should not be allowed to be embezzled, recently sent repeated telegrams to the county government to demand compensation. It is now learned that the county government has verified that the construction funds of the business school are entirely educational funds and has sent a letter to the Educational Funds Association to discuss handling methods in order to recover the public funds.

Shaoxing

The Capture of Refugees Who Robbed Property: Anchang Town in Shaoxing is a prosperous market town. On the 7th, a large number of more than 100 Hunan refugees arrived. At night, they robbed residents of property in the Pengjiawan area. Mo, the director of the Public Security Bureau, led the police to the area and captured Zhao Zhenqing, Jiang Youzhong, Zhao Maoer, and the women Wang Guilin and Zhao Chen on the 8th. Many stolen goods were also seized.

The Establishment of the Court Construction Project Committee: In the afternoon of the 7th, the Shaoxing Local Branch of the Court held an inaugural meeting for the Shaoxing Court Construction Project Committee. As a result of the meeting, the 26,183 yuan, 1 jiao, 7 fen and 9 li allocated by the High Court for the Shaoxing Court project and the proceeds from the sale of the base were deposited in the Shaoxing China Bank, with the interest used as the committee's funds. Jiang Bingkui was elected as the executive committee member.

Xiaoshan

The Water Conservancy Bureau Rushes to Repair the Xixing River Bank: In order to facilitate passenger and freight crossing, Xiaochang Road has set up a station on the Xixing River to facilitate transportation. However, the embankment there has been in disrepair for many years. During the high tide in mid-July this year, several feet of the embankment were washed away. If repairs are not carried out quickly, the railway will be open to traffic next spring and not only will business be affected but there is also a risk of danger. The Construction Department has ordered the Water Conservancy Bureau to investigate and repair it immediately.

Two Murder Suspects Arrested in Wenyan: The Wenyan Public Security Bureau of Xiaoshan arrested Zhou Fada and Zhou Rixin, two murder suspects from Jiangshan, on the 6th. The suspects killed a Zhang family member this spring. Director Du believed that the case was serious and immediately transferred them to the county court for trial.

Tax Ratio on Cotton: In the vicinity of Shao Xiao Anchang and Gualiu, cotton is produced in many places such as Tangtou and Ma'an, and there are many flower shops. The harvest is still good this year. Recently, when the cotton market opened, in addition to strictly ordering various bureaus to inspect it, the Finance Department has stipulated 67,500 yuan for Anchang and it is heard that the Anchang flower tax is collected by the United Tax Bureau.

Ningbo

Kidnapping and Coercion: The Zhou A Wang family in Langxia Litang, Hou Village, and Chaichangtou, Yuyao County, was suddenly visited by eight or nine bandits holding wooden-cased flashlights on the second night before last. They broke into the house and declared that they wanted 1,000 yuan in cash. If they were not allowed, they would take the son as collateral. A Wang is already fifty years old and only has one very young son who refused to be separated. He pleaded with the bandits not to kidnap his son. As a result, he paid 100 yuan on the spot, and the remaining 300 yuan was limited to be delivered to the Lishan Temple within five days. After the bandits got what they wanted, they fired three shots as a warning and left. Also, Yu Linsheng, a farmer from Baishi Village, Jianyan, Zhenhai, and his son Liangyou who is doing business in Hanzhang have a little savings at home. Unexpectedly, four bandits suddenly broke in the night before last and carried out robbery. After checking, the loss was estimated to be several hundred yuan.

The Change of Director of the Cixi Public Security Bureau: Guan Peng, the Director of the Cixi Public Security Bureau, has been in office for four years and submitted his resignation to the county government last month. Hefei

The New County Magistrate Takes Office: Zhang Wu, the new County Magistrate of Hefei, came to Feifei from the province on the evening of the 2nd and went to the county government at 10:00 AM on the 3rd to take office. Ye Cuiwu, the former County Magistrate, was transferred to Fengtai.

The County Party Department Starts Office: The affairs of the Hefei County Party Department have been suspended for a long time. Zhuang Hongfu and others from the village saw them and fished them out and buried them beside the ditch for half a month. Accomplice Xia Lao Wu is Sentenced: Xia Lao Wu, also known as Xia Dengshan, assisted the murderer in killing a military officer in the Dongguan Fengcai Street of this county a few days ago. Before the Minister of Education Also Acting as Minister Arrives, Department Affairs Will Be Signed by Liu Dabai

The resignation of Jiang Menglin, Minister of Education, has been approved and he left Beijing the day before yesterday. On the 8th, Liu Dabai, the Political Vice Minister of Education, went to the Executive Yuan to ask for instructions. The Course of the Qingdao University Incident

Due to the dismissal of new students who used fake certificates to apply

Expelled 17 people who incited the disturbance, classes have now resumed

Qingdao Correspondence: After the Ministry of Education ordered the abolition of the university preparatory system this year, the qualification restrictions for undergraduate applicants to various universities have become extremely strict. After receiving this order from the ministry, the National Qingdao University had to seriously handle the review of the credentials of the new students admitted this year. As a result, it was discovered that more than 20 people used fake certificates to apply to the school. The school authorities immediately ordered their dismissal without further investigation. These dismissed students went to the school's student union on the evening of the 4th to request assistance. The union convened a temporary general meeting to discuss countermeasures and the attitude to be taken. It was decided to implement a strike starting from the 4th to show resolute support. At the same time, the school authorities also convened a school affairs meeting and resolved the following important matters: 1. Students must go through proper procedures for any request to the school and must not resort to strikes to coerce. An announcement should be made to all students to attend classes immediately. No requests will be considered until classes are resumed. 2. The school's student union was organized without legal procedures, which violates the central regulations and interferes with the school's administration. An announcement should be made to all students to inform them that the current illegal student union and its resolutions are invalid. Before a legal student union is established, any matters related to the school will only be accepted if signed by individuals responsible for them. The school authorities issued an announcement based on the previous resolution, advising all students to attend classes as usual and not to take any excessive actions. The majority of the students were willing to obey the school's orders and attend classes as usual. However, the students who used fake certificates joined forces with a few troublemakers to form a disciplinary team, armed with wooden sticks, to prevent classes from starting. The situation was turbulent and almost led to a disaster. The school authorities, fearing that the situation would escalate, convened a school affairs meeting again at 10:00 AM on the 5th. After a long discussion, the following resolutions were reached: 1. Students who used fake certificates, except for those who have voluntarily withdrawn, should have their student status revoked in accordance with the Ministry's regulations and be required to leave the school by 5:00 PM today. The list is attached below. Those who voluntarily withdrew (8 people): Shi Weifan, Li Qianpeng, Tan Mei, Tan Yulan, Huang Yubin, Tang Yuexuan, Liu Jie. Those who were expelled (13 people): Li Jiafan, Wang Jingxi, Cao Shaoming, Wang Boying, Xie Gancai, Fan Ren, Liu Peizhi, Chai Keqing, Yi Eryan, Chen Lezhen, Chen Chaojie, Zhang Guosheng, Zhu Weizhi. 2. The main instigators of this strike incident have been identified as Wang Jingxi, Li Jiafan, Liu Peizhi, Chai Keqing, Ni Eryan, Lu Shiliang, Tang Guanyun, Liu Haigao, Wu Shixun, Sun Tingzhang, Yue Yuan, Hao Lucheng, Cao Wujing, Zhu Baoguang, Shi Xiaoshun, Zheng Shouchong, Yu Hang, and 17 others. In addition to the above two cases being announced separately, an announcement was also made to all students to reassure them to study and not to panic themselves. The incident has subsided and classes have resumed as usual. Yesterday, all faculty members convened a general meeting of all students in the auditorium to give instructions and encourage them to focus on their studies. The situation was excellent. (December 6th)

Annual Meeting of the China Vocational Guidance Organizations Joint Association

To be held in Nanjing on the 14th

The China Vocational Guidance Organizations Joint Association held its inaugural meeting on September 21st at the China Vocational Education Society, as previously reported in this newspaper. The association is scheduled to hold its annual meeting at the Nanjing Municipal Government Auditorium on the 14th of this month (Sunday) at 9:00 AM. The details of the annual meeting are as follows:

Annual Meeting Agenda: (1) Opening and playing music (Nanjing Municipal Government Military Band), (2) All stand in silence, (3) Sing the Party song, (4) Pay the highest respect to the Party, National Flag, and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen, (5) Respectfully read Sun Yat-sen's testament, (6) Opening remarks by the Presidium, (7) Speeches by representatives of various organizations, (8) Lectures (Wu Zhihui, Hu Hanmin, Dai Jitao, Wang Liangchou, Fu Yongzhi, Niu Tiesheng, Cheng Bailu, Gu Yinting), (9) Break (noon). Starting at 1:00 PM in the afternoon, (10) Discussion of proposals (10), (11) Elections (12), (13) Closing remarks by the Chairman, (14) Photography, (15) Adjournment.

Attendees: There are 67 organizations and groups from all over the country, including various social groups, government agencies, universities, vocational schools, and elementary schools with vocational guidance organizations, as well as Nanjing Mayor Wei Daoming, Nanjing Education Bureau Director Zhang Zhongdao, Hu Jiyuan, recommended by the Ministry of Interior, Yang Lian, Director of the Social Education Department, recommended by the Ministry of Education, and others. There are already fifty or sixty registered member representatives. It is reported that the presidium will consist of Zhang Xingzhai, Gao Jiansi, Liu Zhanen, Jiang Wenyu, and Zheng Tonghe.

Various Proposals: (1) Proposals for provincial and municipal education administrative agencies to establish training institutes for vocational guidance personnel or to request universities to establish vocational guidance training classes. (2) The association should publish vocational guidance publications to facilitate its work. (3) Draft of the minimum organization of local vocational guidance centers. (4) Draft of the standard procedures for implementing guidance in vocational guidance centers. (5) Draft of measures for implementing vocational guidance in universities, middle schools, and primary schools. (6) Draft of application forms for vocational guidance. (The above are proposed by the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center.) (7) How should vocational guidance be implemented for apprentices and learners in factories and shops to improve work efficiency and service interest? (8) Determine the minimum funding amount for vocational guidance centers in each city and county. (The above are proposed by the Wuxi County Vocational Guidance Center.) (9) The association should develop a badge design for vocational guidance agencies so that all vocational guidance centers can follow the standard design to produce badges to ensure uniformity and demonstrate cooperation. (10) Should the location and time of the second annual meeting be predetermined? (The above are proposed by the Nanjing Vocational Guidance Center.) (11) The association should compile a detailed statistical report of all the talents registered by the "vocational guidance organizations" of the group members and publicize it nationwide so that factories, companies, and organizations can accurately select the talents they need. (The above is proposed by the China Construction Association.) (12) Vocational guidance should be implemented in elementary schools. (The above is proposed by the Kunshan County Education Bureau.) (13) Request discussion on the establishment of vocational education guidance specialists in provincial, county, and municipal education agencies. (14) Request discussion on cultivating vocational education teachers. (15) Request discussion on advocating the establishment of various professional training institutes. (16) Request discussion on investigating vocational facilities in various countries. (17) Request discussion on expanding vocational education guidance research and publicity. (The above are proposed by the Shanghai County Education Bureau.) (18) Request the Ministry of Education to issue a circular to all levels of schools to vigorously implement vocational guidance. (19) Hold vocational supplementary schools as much as possible. (The above are proposed by Shanghai Municipal Wusong Middle School.) (20) The Vocational Guidance Organizations Joint Association should recommend to the Ministry of Education that the Ministry of Education issue a circular to all provinces to establish vocational guidance centers within a specified time limit. (21) The financial and industrial sectors should cooperate with local vocational guidance agencies to jointly develop new social professions. (The above is proposed by the Changshu Poor Children's Home.) (22) Focus on vocational guidance in rural areas. (23) Conduct pilot unemployment surveys and statistics. (Proposed by Jiangsu Educational Institute)

Division of Responsibilities: The association's office is divided into three departments: General Affairs, Conference Affairs, and Public Relations. The General Affairs Department is responsible for arrangement, documentation, and accounting, and is divided among the Shanghai, Nanjing, and Jiading Vocational Guidance Centers, Jinling University, Nanjing Women's Vocational School, and Jiangsu Education Institute. The Conference Affairs Department is responsible for recording, lecturing, printing, and writing, and is divided among the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center, Provincial Shanghai Middle School, Daxia University, and Hujiang University. The Public Relations Department is responsible for reception and publicity, and is divided among the Shanghai and Nanjing Vocational Guidance Centers, Nanjing Women's Vocational School, and Nanyang Teachers' Reporter Introduction Agency.

Preparatory Office: For the convenience of members and guests, the association has designated the Nanjing Vocational Guidance Center on Qiwang Street in Nanjing as the annual meeting office and the Nanyang Hotel in Confucius Temple as the members' residence. On the 12th, 13th, and 14th, the association will send receptionists to the station with flags to welcome members and guests from all walks of life.
