Free Talk

A Laughing Matter

— Hai Ke

Young Man (at a banquet in a large hotel, after the banquet is over, sees the waiters standing in a row, each holding his coat and hat, waiting) — Seeing them so attentive, like serving upper-class guests, it seems that I can't save a few pennies on this small bill.

A Waiter — Sir, here is your overcoat (helps the young man put it on, and the young man gives him a two-cent ticket).

Another Waiter — Sir, here is your hat (hands it to the young man with both hands, and the young man gives him another two-cent ticket).

Another Waiter — Sir, here are your gloves (hands them to the young man with both hands).

The young man hesitated for a long time and looked at his worn-out gloves) — These... these gloves are not mine. It seems they are not worth even two cents, so you can keep them.

Diner (asking the waiter) — Do you have all kinds of dishes prepared in such a large restaurant?

Waiter — Everything is available, sir, you can order anything you like.

Diner — Then how many varieties are there?

Waiter — There are many varieties. We have four or five different names for each dish.

Father (to his son) — I am a person who has been able to strive since I was a child. By the time I was twenty-five, I was able to stand on my own and be my own master.

Son — But in that year, you married mother and cancelled your master qualifications, didn't you?

Snippets on the International Race Walk

— Shen Zhenchao

The Shanghai International Race Walk covers more than fifty li and is held annually. This is the sixteenth time. This year's event was held on the morning of the 7th. The participants were from six countries: England, Ireland, France, Russia, Portugal, and our China. More than fifty contestants participated. As a result, our country's Zhou Yu Yu and other gentlemen worked hard and bravely won the individual and team championships. Spectators were delighted and overjoyed. Everyone was happy and proud.

The Grandstand Was Full for the First Time The grandstand of the racetrack is crowded with people when watching the grand horse race. This is not surprising. However, it is really a new record to see the International Race Walk so crowded, because the destination of the remote fifty-li journey is in front of the grandstand. Everyone wants to see who will win the championship.

Sacrificing the Warm Quilt to Watch the Race Walk The race walk starts at 8:00 in the morning and ends at the grandstand. The fastest is about 10:30. On weekdays, this time is when Shanghai people are having sweet dreams, but the 7th happened to be a Sunday. To see the athletes' skills, they had to sacrifice their sleep and get up early. There were also many ladies, most of whom did not apply makeup, leaving the true face of beauty. From this, we can also see the enthusiasm of Shanghai people for sports.

Red and White Flags Waving in the Wind The grass in front of the grandstand is the finish line of the race walk. On both sides of the iron fence are flags. The left side is red and the right side is white. All the way to Ma Huo Road Gate, the red and white reflect each other with the green grass that has not withered, which is especially beautiful.

The Ranking Board Announces the Itinerary The race members' itinerary in the field is reported by car at any time and posted on the board. When it was almost 10 o'clock, the board said that China's Zhou Yuyu was the first to reach Hongqiao Road, which was a great comfort to everyone.

Bicycles Participate in the Race Every contestant has a leading staff member who drives a car or rides a bicycle. These fifty contestants are followed by countless bicycle riders. It can be seen that those who are anxious to win are following with bicycles. These dozens of bicycles are no different from joining the competition.

Crowd Celebrates Early Glimpses of People At the intersection of Ma Huo Road and the grandstand, there is a foreign platform. From there, it is very clear to see Weihaiwei Road. The crowds are on this foreign platform. The crowds on both sides of Weihaiwei Road are also crowded and crowded. When it was almost 10:30, cars came one after another. Everyone knew it was coming. There were also those who came to report in advance, saying that Zhou Yuyu was the first. The car left and a large number of bicycles came. So everyone believed it even more. Sure enough, Mr. Zhou shook his hands and feet like a musical beat, and came gracefully. There were about hundreds of people following him. The welcomers on the foreign platform shouted loudly. Mr. Zhou raised his hands to answer, as if saying that I must use it to comfort the people of the country.

People on People Compete to See Heroes After that, Mr. Hou Genren from our country also arrived, in addition to the individual, our country's team championship was six out of ten. Everyone's efforts were indeed raising their eyebrows and cheering for the championship. The audience cheered like thunder. Zhou was surrounded by people on the award platform, so that no water could leak through. There were those who went up on other people's backs to see what Mr. Zhou was like. And the ladies crowded in the crowd, fearing that they would not get a glimpse. When he came out, he followed him again. Mr. Zhou smiled and returned with his many prizes.

Celebrating Success, Sino-Western Duet A military band from the British Army Green Howards was specially invited to the field to add to the fun. When the awards were presented, the military music was melodious to celebrate our success. At the same time, the Chinese also sang loudly. The Sino-Western duet was a beautiful event in the competition.

Wishing Effort to the Old and Young Heroes Among the more than fifty contestants, there were old and young. The Englishman Ross (individual participation) had white hair and must be very old. When he reached the end point, he still worked hard to compete with another teenager, and he took the lead, which is deeply admirable. And Mr. Gong Jintao from our country is only seventeen years old. How should we encourage ourselves in the face of this pair of old and young heroes?

Why Is the Wang Rong Joint European Painting Exhibition Unprecedented?

— Xin Qin

Because they can exhaust the art and all the attached ingenuity.

Yesterday was the second day of the Wang Yachen Rong Joint European Painting Exhibition. The reporter made a special trip to observe it for two hours. Because of his superficial understanding of painting, he dared not comment. Now, he only briefly describes one or two points based on his personal views in order to prove why this meeting is unprecedented. I think it will be welcomed by readers.

Special Venue The venue is the Club of China, a model of newly built Western-style houses. The interior and exterior layout and decoration are extremely rich and magnificent. The three floors are full of precious paintings, which are the culmination of ancient and modern art. It is competent and pleasant. This venue does not fail this meeting, and this meeting does not fail this venue.

Numerous Masterpieces Mr. Wang has always emphasized practicality in his paintings, which cannot be compared with those who wield their pens casually. Mrs. Rong happens to be like-minded with Mr. Wang. The heavenly couple traveled to Europe and traveled north together. They worked together to collect the treasures of ancient and modern art in Europe and the West to share with the Chinese people. There are many dazzling and beautiful things. Who would say it is not appropriate to call them masterpieces?

Outstanding Frames Painters have two things that are most hesitant about: one is the frame, and the other is the printing plate. The frame is especially important for exhibitions. Mr. Wang seems to be aware of this, so half of the frames he uses seem to be brought back from Europe and the West. It is said that half of them are specially entrusted to Hongyuan Art Casting Company in this city to produce. The company was founded by the famous sculptor Zhang Chenbo. Zhang also made a great contribution to the excellence of this frame.

Mei Lanfang returned to China with honors from the United States this autumn. The big axis Mei Lanfang's Su San Qi Jie's sound (bitter) in the curtain has already resounded throughout the hall. Thoughts After Seeing Bi Xiufang's Paintings and Calligraphy

— Diaotu

Chinese art, only calligraphy and painting are worshiped by foreigners. Therefore, countries have exhibitions. Since the Tang and Song dynasties, famous painters have emerged in large numbers. The plum blossoms, orchids, bamboos, and chrysanthemums they painted each have their own specialty. Those who do not have superb calligraphy and outstanding character are not easy to write. Such as Zhu Yuanzhang of Song Dynasty painted plum blossoms, Zheng Suonan painted orchids, Su Dongpo painted bamboo, and Xu Zhongsi painted chrysanthemums. These are all obvious to the eyes. Although there are many later starters, they do not break away from the stereotypes of these four masters. There are occasional casual wielders of the pen, which are even more inferior and not worth mentioning. Today, after seeing Bi Xiufang's calligraphy, true grass, official script, and seal script are combined. His unique running script is based on Zhu Cai Su Huang's above the two old men, which is lovable. Those who know him think that it will be passed on in the future, so the hall pictures, couplets, and fan faces are sold out. The plum blossoms, orchids, bamboos, and chrysanthemums he paints also come from the wonderful place in calligraphy. The strokes use the ancient method, and the supplements of the stones are also positioned properly. The ink is divided into five colors, and the inscription is also fresh and beautiful. As a result, the painters are also too busy to order paintings. I feel relaxed and happy here, and I deeply admire Mr. Bi's decades of hard work and solitary work. This achievement is admired by people from all walks of life, and I cannot help but feel it and say it.

Travel Notes in Southeast Asia (95)

— Linghua

On the tenth day, Zhong Yu Gong led Yu to travel. He rested at the station without a seat. Zhong then called two Burmese people to make them get up and let us two sit. Also, a person was lying on a long bench in his park. He sat on it and gently hit it to wake him up and let me sit. Yu did not agree with this, thinking that it was not a forgiving way. If this happened in China, it would be inevitable to fight for a seat. He replied that this place emphasizes class. As long as we dress in Western clothes and speak English, we can ask Burmese people to give up their seats anywhere. If we meet officials or detectives in the countryside, we must speak English, and everything will be easy. Yu thought that the Burmese people did not dare to compete with others because of the fall of their country. It is also the habit of dyeing India and other places. India originally had four classes, so Buddha transformed it with equal law, but it has not been removed and still exists today. This law cannot be implemented in China in one step, which shows that Chinese people have a true spirit of equality.

The British have the military and political power in Burma, followed by the Indians who have the economic power. India is a large country in Central Asia with many intelligent people and superior business skills, followed by Westerners, and then by Chinese who also have economic power. The next are Burmese officials and merchants, and those who work as coolies belong to the 吉能 people of India. Those who pull rickshaws are all 吉能 people who are black, but the Burmese people in the countryside live in thatched huts and are very poor. According to people, sometimes they don’t have food and only eat porridge to get by.

In the past, geography books said that people in high places are lazy and love to gossip. Burmese people are especially so. They like to give alms and are poor. Most of Siam is also the same. Because of their belief in Buddhism, believing in Buddhism easily makes people lazy, so lazy people mostly believe in Buddhism and like to give alms. The method of giving alms is also worthless. Burmese rich people often give dozens or hundreds of dollars in food items to the Buddha at a time, but they discard them after giving them and do not eat them, thinking that those who offer to the Buddha should not eat them again. This kind of waste of material resources is one of the ten major causes of poverty for Burmese people, which is strange. Also, they do not know how to be frugal and save money. They love to be happy. When they have money, everyone gathers to eat, and the rich give alms without hesitation. Wan Hui Shi said that the Burmese people are Buddhist communists who value wealth and respect. If they know their customs and can speak Burmese, they can easily be welcomed wherever they go. Everyone loves to give alms, so there is communication between the rich and the poor. Their outlook on life is very casual. Because everyone has been a monk, they feel that the family is also an ephemeral thing, unlike Westerners and Chinese who are stingy and contemptuous.

Warmth in My Heart (332)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Sixteen: Cui Xiu Diligently Asks for Words from the Teacher; Heroic Women Talk About War at a Brothel Banquet

The old year has passed, and spring has returned. It is again a new year, a new scene. At that time, the government was promoting the use of the National Calendar. By the end of the old calendar and the beginning of the new year, it was still the same as before. The rich people in Beijing hid in their villas in Tianjin, because they could gamble heavily in the New Year. Those who stayed in Beijing also enjoyed their Lunar New Year entertainment. As for Shanghai, every household set off firecrackers and every place had peach talismans. A whole month was spent in entertainment. The National Calendar's New Year's Day was just a few red newspapers with stories published by the newspapers, and a few red paper lanterns hanging on the government offices and temples, blowing in the wind and rain, just to show the scene. Time flies quickly. In a blink of an eye, the gongs and drums of the New Year have stopped, and the lanterns of the Lantern Festival are also fading. Those brothels have also reached the point of turning around. Green Ripple was scheduled to enter the venue on the eighteenth day of the first month, and her name was changed to Green Ripple. On that day, Zuo Shichen was going to fulfill his obligation to eat all the opening banquets. Not only that, but he also dragged two friends, Long Ziyun and Lin Fanzi. After Zuo Shichen told them about it, they were both willing to help. Long Ziyun originally appreciated Yi's gentle and quietness, saying that this child is promising. Lin Fanzi was originally indifferent. Everyone was happy for a while, and he was also willing to join in the fun. He was a good socializer by nature, and that kind of invitation only had obligations and no rights, and had a bit of a supportive nature. Everyone seemed to have a meaning of "Who is not as good as me in doing good?" He only fulfilled his obligations this time, and there was no precedent for the next time. Therefore, everyone was very happy. They arranged the days. The first day was Zuo Shichen, the second day was Long Ziyun, and the third day was Lin Fanzi. Naturally, Long and Lin were present on the day Zuo Shichen invited guests, and Zuo Shichen was also present on the day Long and Lin invited guests. However, in addition, they invited many slightly polite people. If someone in the audience that day praised this little master, they would say that turning a hall and singing well is like the co-examiners of the rural examination in the past getting a good scroll and rushing to recommend it. Sure enough, there were also those who did not enter the eyes of the chief examiner, but most of them could be admitted. After three days of inviting guests, Green Ripple gained seven or eight households. The place in the small garden used to be inhabited by a Western merchant, and there were some flowers and trees, but it was not easy to find tranquility in the noise in Shanghai. The natural trend of Fuzhou Road and Hankou Road gradually moved to the west. The small garden had long been surrounded by restaurants and singing halls, and it was no longer quiet in the noise. They simply sold the small garden to another Western merchant to build their brothel houses. So that small garden has become a swallow's nest and oriole's nest, and the furnishings in the halls of Shanghai are the most annoying, all the same decoration. From that one to this one, they are all the same type.

Will the Financial Gold Rush Continue Unabated?

Truly frightening… another jump of thirteen taels

Miserable… for the general bears

Breaking the thirty-tael barrier! On December 9th, the gold price once again saw a shockingly high price, presenting a new record unprecedented in history. It surged past the 630-tael mark, a fierce rise of over ten taels. Like ten thousand horses galloping, the momentum was overwhelming. The opening market had a difference of eight taels. However, the pace was swift, with only slight retreats of one or two taels. The overseas silver market's decline slightly eased, showing a slight rebound. Yet, the gold price managed to hold its ground. It was rumored that a certain bank had purchased a substantial amount of spot goods the day before. Upon hearing this, fellow traders were in high spirits. Consequently, major players like Fuchang, Xinxing, Yongheng, Taikang, and Run enthusiastically bought in. However, Shunli, Tongtai, Changyong, and Yongfeng, among others, were selling off, causing the price to soar, rising eight taels. In the afternoon, the Dalian gang and Yongheng Yuancheng Yong, among others, aggressively bought in, mainly because the demand for drafts was even more strained, and the market's edge was truly astonishing. However, the storm was turbulent, with rapid advances and retreats, resulting in a fluctuation of four taels. By the close, the total increase was seven taels. Looking back, the number of transactions was still not large, and the amount per transaction was small. Fellow traders generally maintained a cautious approach, engaging carefully for fear of danger. Ultimately, the peak was reached at 633 taels and five qian. Observing the situation, it is feared that a new era may reappear in the future. Automobile News

Commentary

A Unique Automobile Driver Oath

— Zhizheng

Cleveland Safety Design Committee Creates Ten Commandments for Drivers to Swear to, an Ingenious Way to Reduce Car Accidents

Among the many automobile problems at present, none is more serious than car accidents. Engineering experts in various countries are studying from a mechanical perspective how to reduce dangers. Municipal experts are trying to limit speeding from a municipal perspective. These and other articles published in newspapers are truly countless and magnificent. As the previous issue of this publication contained, "On the Global Road Association Solving the Problem of Car Accidents," it can be said that no effort was spared and everything was taken into consideration. However, in fact, although the laws are strict, the problem of accidents is increasing daily. In Shanghai alone, there were more than 10,000 cases in eleven months, which is extremely shocking. Car accidents are so serious, and the methods everyone comes up with are even more ingenious. Recently, in order to solve the problem of car accidents, the Cleveland City Government in the United States specially organized a Safety Design Committee. What is the committee's plan? It's actually quite interesting: it has formulated ten articles of faith, requiring each car driver to sign, obey, and swear to abide by them. These ten articles of faith are important conditions for preventing car accidents. After each car driver swears, it is stored in the committee for safekeeping. It is said that in this way, car accidents have indeed been reduced greatly. These ten sworn articles of faith are listed as follows:

(1) When I am driving, I will only act as half of the people in the world, who are deaf and blind, and their safety must be maintained by me. What is the idea of this article of faith? It is to correct the current car drivers' impatience. When driving, they stare at everything and drive at full speed, or they clearly see that there are many people in front of them, but they always think that they must give way, so they are not willing to reduce their speed and proceed calmly. Now, they are told to think that half of the people in the world are deaf and blind, and drivers will naturally be extra careful.

(2) When I am driving, I must pay special attention and stop immediately in case of danger. This article seems very simple, but it also has deep meaning. Because most drivers now cannot concentrate on being careful, they secretly drive their vehicles. When danger occurs, it is naturally too late to brake, and accidents therefore occur and cannot be remedied. If every driver can concentrate on driving and stop immediately in case of danger, the problem of accidents can be solved.

(3) I swear to respect the rights of other drivers and pedestrians and obey the road laws. The biggest drawback of drivers is that they are arrogant and think that only they are the most honorable. Therefore, they do not care about pedestrians and have no courtesy towards other drivers. Accidents therefore arise. Therefore, the United States is now promoting "Road Courtesy," which is exactly this meaning. If everyone is courteous, all problems can be solved.

(4) At intersections, schools, and other areas that require special attention, I must reduce my speed so that I can stop at any time. Intersections are the most accident-prone places, especially in prosperous areas, where car collisions occur frequently. The reason is nothing more than the unwillingness to reduce speed and driving recklessly. As a result, when an accident occurs, it is too late to avoid it, so extra care is needed in these places.

(5) I swear not to regard cars as toys. The main cause of car accidents is that drivers are unwilling to be cautious. They mostly regard cars as toys, circling around and climbing mountains, thinking that it is a kind of game. How can they not have accidents? Therefore, to remedy this, drivers must swear that they will no longer take cars as toys.

(6) When I am parking or turning, I must first turn on the lights. Car signals are originally very simple. They only have the red light on the back, which is the most important. However, many drivers inadvertently ignore even just one red light. Parking and turning are the most important. If the red light is not turned on, the vehicles behind cannot be notified, and collisions are inevitable.

(7) I must drive on the right side of the road and obey the police's instructions. In Europe and the United States, driving is on the right side of the road. In China, it is on the left side of the road. The right side and the left side are not the problem. Only obedience is the most important. In big cities, the right-hand rule can still work. Once in the countryside, cars act completely freely and no longer care about what is left and right. Therefore, the most serious accidents do not occur in major cities but on remote highways. The reason is the same: obeying the police's instructions is even more important; otherwise, it will completely fall into disorder.

(8) When the weather is bad, I must drive with special caution. Not to mention anything else, just foggy weather is enough. Everything becomes blurred. When two cars drive towards each other, a collision will occur immediately with one careless move. The same is true for snowy weather.

(9) I swear to abide by the traffic laws. Although traffic laws cannot be said to completely eliminate accidents, if they are conscientiously obeyed, they can ultimately achieve considerable effectiveness. We examine the causes of car accidents. Violating traffic laws is also an important component. Therefore, if cars can strictly abide by traffic laws, it can be said to be a good medicine that treats the symptoms.

(10) When reversing, I must first see clearly behind me. Accidents caused by reversing are also not uncommon. Most of them occur because they did not see clearly whether there were pedestrians and vehicles behind them before reversing. As a result, people only pay attention to the vehicles coming from the front but do not suspect that the vehicle behind them is reversing. Therefore, this matter seems very small, but the impact is quite large.

From the above, the ten articles of faith formulated by the Cleveland Safety Design Committee, although unusually simple, used to be seen by car drivers as uninteresting in the past. Now, car drivers swear to abide by them, changing from passive to active, and its effect is naturally different from those who are regarded as irrelevant.

Ratio of Cars to People in the World

— Lin

There are 35 million cars in the world, with one car for every 55 people.

According to a survey by the United States Department of Commerce, in 1929, the number of cars in the world exceeded 35,000,000. The survey included 157 countries, territories, and regions. The total number of registered passenger cars, freight cars, and buses in the world was 35,127,389, an increase of 3,092,826 or 9 percent compared to the beginning of 1929. The number of cars on the roads in various countries around the world is increasing daily. In 1922, the total was 12,530,416, which increased to 155 percent by 1929.

At the beginning of 1930, with a world population of 1,949,000,000, there was one car for every 55 people. In 1929, the number was one car for every 61 people. In the United States, according to the latest statistics, there is one car for every 4.5 people. A year ago, there was one car for every 4.87 people. Outside the United States, there is one car for every 216 people. At the beginning of 1929, there was one car for every 247 people.

Canada and New Zealand's car-to-population ratio is slightly lower than that of the United States, ranking second, with one car for every eight people. Australia ranks third, with one car for every ten people. Monaco is fourth, with one car for every sixteen people. In Yemen, in southwestern Arabia, there is only one car for every 104,166 people. In Ethiopia, there is one car for every 17,781 people. In Afghanistan, there is one car for every 17,778 people. The above-mentioned latest statistics show increases in East, West, South Africa, China, Persia, Syria, and Siam. Other smaller countries have seen slightly more car sales opportunities recently.

According to the latest car statistics, the number of registered cars of various styles in the continental United States reached 26,653,450, which is three times more than in foreign countries. In the United States alone, the number of registered passenger cars accounted for 78 percent of the world's total, and commercial vehicles accounted for 62 percent of the total. France ranks second in the total number, followed by England and Canada. Among the countries with cars in the world, Oman, a southwestern Arab territory, and Bermuda, a British territory, have only ten registered cars, ranking last.

Page 20

The number of commercial vehicles registered worldwide is greater than that of passenger cars. In 1929, the number of passenger cars registered worldwide increased by 2,540,511 or 9.4 percent, while the number of freight cars and buses increased by 552,315 or 10.9 percent. Therefore, the number of passenger cars increased by 7.3 percent compared to the increase in 1928, while freight cars and buses decreased by 0.1 percent.

The number of passenger cars in most countries is greater than that of freight cars. However, in some countries, the number of commercial vehicles exceeds that of passenger cars, and these commercial vehicles can open up remote areas, leading the way for the use of passenger cars. In 1929, the number of car registrations in the United States increased by 2,026,527 or 8.2 percent, compared to an increase of 1,367,738 or 5.9 percent in the previous year. Outside the United States, the increase in cars in 1929 was 1,069,297 or 14.40 percent, compared to 973,347 or 15.1 percent in 1928.

Anecdotes

The Honor of the Morris Cowley

— Yun

It is difficult to travel the 8,000 miles from Cape Town to Cairo, the capital of Egypt, due to road repairs and obstacles. Now, a 1924 Morris Cowley convertible has uniquely completed this long-distance journey and is the first standard British vehicle to create this record. It is commendable and worthy of praise that the drivers, Miss Bairche and Miss White Gil, are the first successful women to achieve this.

Miss Bairche and Miss White set off from Cape Town on April 1, taking the route through Johannesburg, Nairobi, Juba, and Aswan towards Cairo. On the way, the Rhodesian mountains were flooded, and the car could not move forward, delaying them for seven weeks. When they arrived at Carl Ferry, they were delayed again for more than ten days. They finally arrived safely in Cairo on September 15, taking a total of five and a half months. They then went from Alexandria to Marseille, through Calais, to England on September 29. Sir William hosted a banquet at the Morris factory to welcome them wholeheartedly. Sir William was the first to sign the ladies' diaries when they set off from Cape Town. He was also one of the last to sign, as he signed the book again upon completion of the journey to congratulate them on their success. It is said that this car never needed to be repaired throughout the journey, and the reputation of the Morris car was greatly enhanced. In October, the number of daily visitors to the Morris car's London sales office was overwhelming, like the scenery on the Shanyin Road.

Calligraphy and Painting News

Painter Yi Lu Chen Yichan declares that his name is Zepei, his style name is Rongsheng, he is a lover of epigraphy, and also a painter and zen practitioner. He is from eastern Sichuan. In his youth, he abandoned his pen to study, rich in strategy. He has experienced hardships during the revolutionary service for twenty years. Many generals in Sichuan and Yunnan came from his school. He has the style of a Confucian general. In the middle, he has traveled to famous mountains and rivers at home and abroad, paying attention everywhere. He has specialized in studying the six methods for ten years. His pen is a teacher of nature, and the strange energy in his chest is expressed in calligraphy and painting. Those who get it treasure it. In recent years, he has returned to studying Buddhist teachings and paintings to participate in Zen. He has cultivated his mind in the quiet Kuanglu for two winters and summers, sketching the scenery and creating a grand view. The help of Jiangshan has its own origin. Female Guan Hua is also skilled in landscape painting. The family's calligraphy and painting have recently moved to Shanghai. Her works of Lushan scenery have collected dozens of pieces and will be screened soon. The painter uses the brush of seal script to write the spirit of nature, which is enough to open a new era for Chinese painting. Yu Youren, Wang Yiting, Jiang Boqi, Huang Shihong, Li Liejun, Fang Shengtao, Jia Yao, Zhang Shanzi, Zhang Daqian, Wang Dungen and other gentlemen have made reservations and introduced the remuneration to the world, they say.
